            function applyStateChangeToField(state, $field) {
              var values = getWizardActionValues($field);
              var properties = $field.attr('data-wizard-action');
              _.each(values, function(value, i) {
                var re = new RegExp('\\$value' + (i + 1), 'g');
                properties = properties.replace(re, value);
              });
              state.set(JSON.parse(properties));
            }
            function getWizardActionValues($field) {
              if ($field.attr('type') == 'checkbox') {
                return [$field.is(':checked').toString()];
              }
              else if ($field.val()) {
                return $field.val().split(':');
              }
              else {
                return [''];
              }
            }

            function isExperimentEnabled(id) {
              return typeof corewizard.masterconfig !== 'undefined'
                && typeof corewizard.masterconfig.abacus !== 'undefined'
                && typeof corewizard.masterconfig.abacus[id] !== 'undefined'
                && corewizard.masterconfig.abacus[id] !== '0';
            }

            if (corewizard.core.model.get('tab') == "opensearch") {
              	corewizard.core.$wizardFormWrapper.find('input')
                  .each(function(index, element) {
                    applyStateChangeToField(corewizard.core.state,$(element));
                  });
            }

            corewizard.core.submit();
        });

        $(function() {
            corewizard.applyCarouselOmniture();
        });

                        } else if (typeof(element.style.backgroundImage) === 'undefined' || element.style.backgroundImage.indexOf(slotConfig.url) === -1) {
                            element.setAttribute('data-src', slotConfig.url);
                            element.style.backgroundImage = 'url(' + slotConfig.url + ')';
                            element.style.backgroundRepeat = 'no-repeat';
                            element.style.backgroundSize = 'cover';
                            element.setAttribute('alt', slotConfig.altText);
                        }
                    }
                },
                loadActiveMarquee = function () {
                    var slots = window.expads.slots.MARQUEE.adDefault.adCalls[expads.slots.MARQUEE.adToLoad].slots,
                        slotKey;
                    for (slotKey in slots) {
                        if (slots.hasOwnProperty(slotKey)) {
                            displayFallbackImage(slots[slotKey]);
                        }
                    }
                };
            window.expads = window.expads || {};
            window.expads.initialize = window.expads.initialize || loadActiveMarquee;
            window.expads.refresh = window.expads.refresh || function (targetingObject, adToLoad) {
                    window.expads.slots.MARQUEE.adToLoad = adToLoad;
                    loadActiveMarquee();
                };
            return window.expads;
        });
    }
})(window);

</script>

  window.alertMenuClickHandlers = {
    flightMIPGT: function(){
        if (window.AlertsMenu) {
            AlertsMenu.sendeVar28('Header.Notif.LX.Flight.GT');
        }
    },

    flightMIPActivity: function(){
        if (window.AlertsMenu) {
            AlertsMenu.sendeVar28('Header.Notif.LX.Flight.Activity');
        }
    },

    spSignIn: function(e, alertItemRef) {
        if (window.AlertsMenu) {
            AlertsMenu.sendeVar28('Header.Notif.SP.SignIn');
        }
    },
    spNudgeEnroll: function(e, alertItemRef) {
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();

        var $target = $(e.target).closest('.alert-item');

        $target
            .find('.close-button')
            .remove();

        $target
            .find('.alert-message')
            .html('You are receiving price updates for your recently saved and viewed items. Watch your inbox!');

        if (Scratchpad.state.loggedInUser) {
            uitk.utils.liveAnnounce('You are receiving price updates for your recently saved and viewed items. Watch your inbox!');
        }

        if (window.uitk
        && window.uitk.utils
        && window.uitk.utils.focusElement) {
            uitk.utils.focusElement($target);
        }

        if (window.AlertsMenu) AlertsMenu.sendeVar28('Header.Notif.SP.OptIn');
        if (window.Scratchpad) Scratchpad.enrollInNudge();
    },
    spBasicNews: function(e, alertItemRef) {
        if (window.AlertsMenu) {
            AlertsMenu.sendeVar28('Header.Notif.SP.News');
        }
    },
    spDetailedNews: function(e, alertItemRef) {
        if (window.AlertsMenu) {
            AlertsMenu.sendeVar28('Header.Notif.SP.LiveAlerts');
        }
    }
  };

   /*===========Accessible Strings============*/

  window.accessibleBadgeMessagePlural = "You have {0} notifications";
  window.accessibleNotifClose = "Close";
</script>

<script>
$(function() {
  var $moreMenu = $('.site-header.site-header-secondary > .header-navigation-menu > .site-navigation .new-more-menu');
  var $vlinks = $('.site-header.site-header-secondary > .header-navigation-menu > .site-navigation > ul.utility-nav');
  var $hlinks = $('#hlinks');

  var numOfItems = 0;
  var totalSpace = 0;
  var breakWidths = [];

  // Get initial state
  $vlinks.children("li").outerWidth(function(i, w) {
    totalSpace += w;
    numOfItems += 1;
    breakWidths.push(totalSpace);
  });

  var availableSpace, numOfVisibleItems, requiredSpace;

  function check() {
    // Get instant state
    availableSpace = $vlinks.width() - 65;
    numOfVisibleItems = $vlinks.children("li").length;
    requiredSpace = breakWidths[numOfVisibleItems - 1];

    // There is not enough space
    if (requiredSpace > availableSpace) {
      while(requiredSpace > availableSpace) {
        $vlinks.children("li").last().prependTo($hlinks);
        numOfVisibleItems -= 1;
        requiredSpace = breakWidths[numOfVisibleItems - 1];
      }
    // There is more than enough space
    } else if (availableSpace > breakWidths[numOfVisibleItems]) {
      while(availableSpace > breakWidths[numOfVisibleItems] && numOfVisibleItems <= numOfItems) {
        $hlinks.children().first().appendTo($vlinks);
        numOfVisibleItems++;
      }
    }
    // Update the menu accordingly
    if (numOfVisibleItems >= numOfItems) {
      $moreMenu.addClass('visuallyhidden');
    } else $moreMenu.removeClass('visuallyhidden');
  }

  // Window listeners
  $(window).resize(function() {
    check();
  });

  check();
});
</script>
